Title
===
Job Listing Scraper 


## Install & Dependence
- NodeJS
- Puppeteer
- aws-sdk


## Dataset Preparation
| Dataset | Download |
| ---     | ---   |
| dataset-A | [download]() |
| dataset-B | [download]() |
| dataset-C | [download]() |

## Use
- for train
  ```
  python train.py
  ```
- for test
  ```
  python test.py
  ```
## Pretrained model
| Model | Download |
| ---     | ---   |
| Model-1 | [download]() |
| Model-2 | [download]() |
| Model-3 | [download]() |
